. * anticipated regret: Anticipated regret was measure
> d by two items. If I take a Corona vaccine, I might 
> regret it./If I do NOT take a Corona vaccine, I migh
> t regret it. The score on the first item was subtrac
> ted from the score of the second item to achieve a m
> easure of net-anticipated regret. Item construction 
> was in accordance with Brewer et al. (2016) specific
> ation of anticipated regret measures.
. pwcorr fomo1 fomo2, sig

             |    fomo1    fomo2
-------------+------------------
       fomo1 |   1.0000 
             |
             |
       fomo2 |  -0.3889   1.0000 
             |   0.0000
             |
. gen net_anticipated_regret = fomo2-fomo1
.

. *Table S10.     Heterogeneous effects: Vector
. foreach var of global heterogeneous_PAP {
  2. reg intent_vector $w1_treatments `var' `var'_w1_t2 `var'_w1_t3  $control if wave == 1, rob
  3. testparm `var'_w1_t2 `var' w1_t2
  4. local F1 = r(p)
  5. testparm `var'_w1_t3 `var' w1_t3
  6. local F2 = r(p)
  7. outreg2 using "$working_ANALYSIS/results/tables/TableS10_heterogeneous_intention_vector", drop($control) addstat("Interaction: T1 sig.", `F1', "I
> nteraction: T2 sig.", `F2') adec(3) word  adjr2 dec(2)
  8. }

. *Table S18.     Heterogeneous treatment effects as pre-registered
. foreach var of global heterogeneous_PAP_lagged {
  2. reg no_action $treatments `var' `var'_t2 `var'_t3 `var'_t4 $control, rob
  3. testparm `var'_t2 `var' t2
  4. local F1 = r(p)
  5. testparm `var'_t3 `var' t3
  6. local F2 = r(p)
  7. testparm `var'_t4 `var' t4
  8. local F3 = r(p)
  9. outreg2 using "$working_ANALYSIS/results/tables/TableS18_vaccine_hesitancy_heterogeneous", drop($control) addstat("Interaction: T1 sig.", `F1', "

. do "$working_ANALYSIS/scripts/03_robustness_checks_no_exclusion.do"

. *--------------------------------------------------------------------
. * SCRIPT: 03_robustness_checks_no_exclusion.do
. * PURPOSE: This file runs the main analysis using the whole sample without any exclusion criterias.
. *--------------------------------------------------------------------
. 
. 
. *Load dataset without applying the exlcusion criteria
. use "$working_ANALYSIS/processed/corona_ger_ROBUSTNESS", clear 
(corona-ger-w1)

. 
. 
. *Setting variable lists
. {
. *globals for excludion check
. global selective_exclusion ///
> /*socio-econ*/ female age1 age2 age3 age4 age5 edu1 edu2 edu3 edu4 adj_hh_income married ///
> /*explanatory*/ denied_vaccine_past c19_risk_index NA net_anticipated_regret dogmatism /// 
> /*outcome variables*/ intent_mrna intent_vector confidence_mrna confidence_vector constraints complacency calculation collective no_action 
. 
. global w1_treatments w1_t2 w1_t3
. global treatments t2 t3 t4
. global control female i.age_grps i.edu adj_hh_income married //as specified in PAP)
. global five_c confidence_mrna confidence_vector complacency constraints calculation collective
. global five_c_lagged l_confidence_mrna l_confidence_vector l_complacency l_constraints l_calculation l_collective
. global x_2 no_action denied_vaccine_past z_c19_risk_index z_NA z_net_anticipated_regret z_dogmatism
. global x_2_lagged l_no_action l_denied_vaccine_past z_l_c19_risk_index z_l_NA z_l_net_anticipated_regret z_l_dogmatism
. 
. *globals for heterogeneous effects
. global heterogeneous_PAP no_action denied_vaccine_past z_c19_risk_index z_NA z_net_anticipated_regret z_dogmatism 
. global heterogeneous_PAP_lagged l_no_action l_denied_vaccine_past z_l_c19_risk_index z_l_NA z_l_net_anticipated_regret z_l_dogmatism
. }

. 
. *Table S2.      Balance table: Main sample and excluded
. iebaltab $selective_exclusion if wave == 1, grpvar(excluded2) rowvarlabels save("$working_ANALYSIS/results/tables/TableS2_excluded_vs_nonexcluded")
